    narrative: ### üåë Session 1: The Phobos Routine

The gate swallows you like it always does‚Äîcold first, then nothing, then everything.

The transition lasts exactly 3.7 seconds. You know this because you've counted it twelve times. The purple light peels away from your skin like static discharge, and then there it is: the **Phobos Dungeon**, laid out before you in all its underwhelming, E-Rank glory.
